So you can arrange the song in a creative way and create and publish your own interpretations.\r\nMany of the midi files are free (for example: Mutopia Project with tousends of songs), others are copyright protected and have to be purchased.\r\nThe SoundDesigner Music Creator contains a collection of 4 synthesizer engines: GM Bank, Additive Synthesizer, Waveform Modulator and Sampler. It can also import preset sounds from the SoundDesigner and the Dynamic Synth and sound samples. First steps:\r\n1) Load a midi file (or a project).\r\n2) Assign sounds to the different tracks. (Select a track and then select the sounds).\r\n3) Test (play) the track and than test the whole song (play all).\r\n4) If you want, you can add special effects to the tracks (optional).\r\n5) Play or They are based on the same principles as Ishihara plates used by optometrists, but use test plates that are randomly and accurately generated at run time.  This is different from many other tests using scanned or static images that can be grossly inaccurate.  \r\n \r\nThe prevalence of color vision deficiency is about 5%. Most of them are caused by the missing or defect of one of the three cones in the retina responsible for color vision. If one cone is missing, it is called dichromacy which has three types corresponding to the three cones (protanopia, deuteranopia, tritanopia to L-, M-, S-cone respectively).
